CPGE.floorObject=function(obj){ obj.onFloor=false; obj.onWall=false; obj.onSpring=false; obj.addTick(function(time){ this.onFloor=false; this.onWall=false; this.onSpring=false; var block; var right=[this.position[0]+this.size[0]/2,this.position[1]]; var left=[this.position[0]-this.size[0]/2,this.position[1]]; var top=[this.position[0],this.position[1]-this.size[1]/2]; //check if against wall block=this.game.map.environment.blockAt(left[0],left[1]); if((block[0]&CPGE.SOLID)==CPGE.SOLID){ this.position[0]=this.position[0]+(block[1]+block[3]); this.onWall=true; } block=this.game.map.environment.blockAt(right[0],right[1]); if((block[0]&CPGE.SOLID)==CPGE.SOLID){ this.position[0]=this.position[0]+block[1]; this.onWall=true; } //check the bottom this.view.target[0]=x-this.view.size[0]/2; else if(x(this.size[0]-this.view.size[0]/2)) this.view.target[0]=this.size[0]-this.view.size[0]; if(y>this.view.size[1]/2 && y<(this.size[1]-this.view.size[1]/2)) this.view.target[1]=y-this.view.size[1]/2; else if(y(this.size[1]-this.view.size[1]/2)) this.view.target[1]=this.size[1]-this.view.size[1]; }, //returns a sprite newframe=0; this.frame=0; } else if(newframe>=this.states[this.state].frames) { if(this.states[this.state].loop){ newframe=newframe%(this.states[this.state].frames); }else{ newframe=this.states[this.state].frames-1; } } if(newframe!=this.frame){ this.frame=newframe; } //set the last time so we know when this was last called this.lasttime=time; } else if(this.nextstate){
